  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_cd647e4c-440c-4183-af8c-d41b0ef0710d'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer11176967317038624206"><b>Cinderella goes to the con in this fandom-fueled twist on the classic fairy tale.</b><br/><br/>Part romance, part love letter to nerd culture, and all totally adorbs, Geekerella is a fairy tale for anyone who believes in the magic of fandom. Geek girl Elle Wittimer lives and breathes <i>Starfield</i>, the classic sci-fi series she grew up watching with her late father. So when she sees a cospl</span>
  <span id="freeText11176967317038624206" style="display:none"><b>Cinderella goes to the con in this fandom-fueled twist on the classic fairy tale.</b><br /><br />Part romance, part love letter to nerd culture, and all totally adorbs, Geekerella is a fairy tale for anyone who believes in the magic of fandom. Geek girl Elle Wittimer lives and breathes <i>Starfield</i>, the classic sci-fi series she grew up watching with her late father. So when she sees a cosplay contest for a new <i>Starfield</i> movie, she has to enter. The prize? An invitation to the ExcelsiCon Cosplay Ball, and a meet-and-greet with the actor slated to play Federation Prince Carmindor in the reboot. With savings from her gig at the Magic Pumpkin food truck (and her dad’s old costume), Elle’s determined to win…unless her stepsisters get there first.<br /> <br />Teen actor Darien Freeman used to live for cons—before he was famous. Now they’re nothing but autographs and awkward meet-and-greets. Playing Carmindor is all he’s ever wanted, but the <i>Starfield</i> fandom has written him off as just another dumb heartthrob. As ExcelsiCon draws near, Darien feels more and more like a fake—until he meets a girl who shows him otherwise.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11176967317038624206" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

<div id="review_2291389989" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2291389989" />
    <a title="Maria" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/77602709-maria"><img alt="Maria" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519184646p2/77602709.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2291389989?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria" href="/user/show/77602709-maria">Maria</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/77602709-maria?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2291389989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4068577960494264578"><b>5</b>/5 Stars ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️<br/><br/><blockquote> “Never give up on your dreams, and never let anyone tell you that what you love is inconsequential or useless or a waste of time. Because if you love it? If that OTP or children's card game or abridged series or YA book or animated series makes you happy?<br/>That is never a waste of time. Because in the end we're all just a bunch of weirdos standing in front of other weirdos, asking for their username.” <br/><br/>― Ashley Poston, Geekerella </blockquote><br/><br/>GUYS THIS BOOK THIS BOOK! I'M CRYING RIGHT N</span>
  <span id="freeText4068577960494264578" style="display:none"><b>5</b>/5 Stars ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️<br /><br /><blockquote> “Never give up on your dreams, and never let anyone tell you that what you love is inconsequential or useless or a waste of time. Because if you love it? If that OTP or children's card game or abridged series or YA book or animated series makes you happy?<br />That is never a waste of time. Because in the end we're all just a bunch of weirdos standing in front of other weirdos, asking for their username.” <br /><br />― Ashley Poston, Geekerella </blockquote><br /><br />GUYS THIS BOOK THIS BOOK! I'M CRYING RIGHT NOW OF THE FEELS AND I NEVER CRY BECAUSE OF BOOKS! NEVER!<br /><br />This book is perfect. There's no flaw about it! Hence the 5 star rating. It's perfect and relatable and amazing and funny and spectacular and everything I need from a book. This book is for us, geeks. NO ONE WHO ISN'T A GEEK CAN APPRECIATE THIS BOOK THE RIGHT WAY I'M TELLING YOU. No offense to non-geek people but this is a little something for us forever-and-ever geeks.<br /><br />This book is a Cinderella retelling (but could stand out as its own book without the Cinderella influence) about a girl named Ella and her passion for a tv show called "Starfield" (which mostly reminds me of Star Trek and I love that) that she shared with her late father. She lives with her evil stepmother (stepMOnster) and her stepsisters who bully her into existence. After a while she finds out about a contest centering the new film reboot of "Starfield" and she has to enter but at what cost? <br /><br />I've been a geek my entire life. I don't remember myself not being a geek. From Harry Potter to Star Wars to Doctor Who to Marvel to Lord of the Rings... I've been in fandoms my entire life, I've been reading fan fiction my entire life, I've had OTPs I would die for my entire life, I've been making GIFs for my favorite shows for Tumblr my entire life. This book was a hymn to people like me. This book didn't make me cry because of the romance but because of the nerd culture love it portrayed. It made me feel like I belong in an amazing world not too many people can understand. But the ones that can, know. We all geeks know. The author did an amazing job with making us nerds relate to this book cause she's a nerd herself. And she knows. Like for God's sake this book even contained MEMES. FUCKING MEMES. I live for this book.<br /><br />I'm so happy I got to read this. I'm so happy for these characters. I'm so happy they got what they deserved-happiness. I'm happy for Elle, Darien, Sage, Cal, Gail, Lenny, they were all wonderful. And I'm so grateful to the author for giving this book to us. IT'S MY FAVORITE BOOK RIGHT NOW OKAY IT IS. Unless I read another book of hers, or another book about fandom culture and die again. <br /><br />This review is such a mess but I am a mess right now! I would recommend this book a 148394820% to geeks like me, to fandom people like me, to people who know. If you know what I'm talking about throughout this review and if you can understand my feelings for this book then it's for you. Order it, read it and then thank me cause I recommended it this book to you ha! NOW ABOUT TO CRY SOME MORE BYE!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2004037557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4251122164087385404"><b>Oh this was super cute!</b> And an excellent reason for me to stop judging covers because this waaaaay exceeded my expectations from that cover. Live and learn, Cait. LIVE AND LEARN. <b>It was so absolutely heartfelt, that I just...I can't even??</b> It reminded me of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16068905.Fangirl' title='Fangirl by Rainbow Rowell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fangirl</a> all squished with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26365537.Kindred_Spirits' title='Kindred Spirits by Rainbow Rowell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kindred Spirits</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28245707.Queens_of_Geek' title='Queens of Geek by Jen Wilde' rel='nofollow noopener'>Queens of Geek</a> and I <i>loved</i> it. NERDOM APPRECIATION FOR THE WIN.<br/><br/><b>Now I assume the fandom they were cult following was like a Star Wars spin off?</b> Maybe?? I wouldn't have a clue, not knowing anything </span>
  <span id="freeText4251122164087385404" style="display:none"><b>Oh this was super cute!</b> And an excellent reason for me to stop judging covers because this waaaaay exceeded my expectations from that cover. Live and learn, Cait. LIVE AND LEARN. <b>It was so absolutely heartfelt, that I just...I can't even??</b> It reminded me of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16068905.Fangirl" title="Fangirl by Rainbow Rowell" rel="nofollow noopener">Fangirl</a> all squished with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26365537.Kindred_Spirits" title="Kindred Spirits by Rainbow Rowell" rel="nofollow noopener">Kindred Spirits</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/28245707.Queens_of_Geek" title="Queens of Geek by Jen Wilde" rel="nofollow noopener">Queens of Geek</a> and I <i>loved</i> it. NERDOM APPRECIATION FOR THE WIN.<br /><br /><b>Now I assume the fandom they were cult following was like a Star Wars spin off?</b> Maybe?? I wouldn't have a clue, not knowing anything about Star Wars except Darth Vadar is someone's father. <i>However</i>, that didn't impede my enjoyment at all. And I think that's something really special about this book: it's just a love letter to fans and geeks of all types. There's no such thing as "fake fans" here. There's no fan hating! (Although it does note the "monster fans" as Darien calls them, who like will kiss-attack an actor on stage which is 5000% inappropriate for sure and pls stop to those sorts of fans.)<br /><br /><b>I reeeeally loved the Cinderella twist too!</b> The BEST twist was how the "pumpkin" was actually a vegan food truck. Like yes please and thank you?! I'm totally here for how quirky that is. The only downside to the retelling twists though, is that the step-mum and sisters were SUCH caricatures and it was really hard to take that part of the story seriously. <b>I really had no feelings about it?</b> It was just bleh bleh I'm not sure why Elle didn't try to get herself out of the situation.<br /><br /><b>I looooved Darien so so much though.</b> He was THE CUTEST DORK. And like he's doing this reboot for a SUPER famous cult-followed show and he loves it, but everyone assumes he's a vapid jerk in for the money. And really he's scared and anxious and having 399 identity crises per day. &lt;3 He was so precious. <b>I also love his and Elle's relationship growing via text.</b> Shoutout to internet friends who aren't axe murders. WE LOVE YOU.<br /><br />I do think their friendship turned to romance a <i>little</i> fast...especially when they only knew each other via text? And hadn't even really talked deeply??? <b>But the book is only like 320 pages. So.</b><br /><br /><b>I can't even with myself and how many adorakable nerdy contemporaries I'm reading at the moment.</b> I AM USUALLY ALL FOR DRAGON FIRE. But I'm so so so glad I tried this because it just made me so happy! It was deep and there were complex emotions going on there and Darien is the sweetest. <b>And I <i>loved</i> how it underlined that super important message of: pls stop JUDGING PEOPLE YOU DON'T KNOW. </b>You can never know the full story when you don't know someone. Be kind. Listen. Learn. <br /><br />Also be a geek. The geek life is 500% better.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2006938358" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17238852518335152536">So. Much. Fun. <br/><br/>This super cute Cinderella-goes-to-Geeky-Con story is probably closer to a 3.5 in terms of merit because I think it could have been even better <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ pretty much all the adults are terrible, the emotional beats could have been stronger, and a major issue with sticking so closely to your source material is that it becomes fairly predictable. Its sparks back to life once Elle arrives at the Con, though <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but it is such a cute and enjoyable read, it gets roun</span>
  <span id="freeText17238852518335152536" style="display:none">So. Much. Fun. <br /><br />This super cute Cinderella-goes-to-Geeky-Con story is probably closer to a 3.5 in terms of merit because I think it could have been even better <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ pretty much all the adults are terrible, the emotional beats could have been stronger, and a major issue with sticking so closely to your source material is that it becomes fairly predictable. Its sparks back to life once Elle arrives at the Con, though <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but it is such a cute and enjoyable read, it gets rounded up to 4 stars!<br /><br />Please ignore the terrible cover art and pick this up if you've ever gotten excited when you saw someone wearing a tee-shirt referencing a movie/book/band you like, or if your heart secretly melts over meet-cute romances, or if you enjoy, you know, SMILING ABOUT ADORABLE THINGS.<br /><br />Review to come. I'm still grinning from ear to ear. :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="17238852518335152536" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2363050032" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2363050032" />
    <a title="High Lady of The Night Court" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court"><img alt="High Lady of The Night Court" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556501727p2/62560505.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2363050032?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="High Lady of The Night Court" class="user" itemprop="url" name="High Lady of The Night Court" href="/user/show/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court">High Lady of The Night Court</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court?shelf=contemporary-read">contemporary-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2363050032" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7658723500234589556"><b>
  <i>“We’re all geeks here”</i>
</b><br/><br/>A love story most unlikely, a friendship most unexpected and a story inevitably beautiful. The horrors of being tied to a stepmom who hates you. The shackles that come along with fame. The tug of the familiar, the nervousness of taking risks. I can't help but fall in love with dreams.<br/><br/>In this book we follow two characters, Danielle Wittimer who is the biggest fan of the Starfield series and grew up with it, and Darien a teen actor who just scored the lead role in the rem</span>
  <span id="freeText7658723500234589556" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“We’re all geeks here”</i>
</b><br /><br />A love story most unlikely, a friendship most unexpected and a story inevitably beautiful. The horrors of being tied to a stepmom who hates you. The shackles that come along with fame. The tug of the familiar, the nervousness of taking risks. I can't help but fall in love with dreams.<br /><br />In this book we follow two characters, Danielle Wittimer who is the biggest fan of the Starfield series and grew up with it, and Darien a teen actor who just scored the lead role in the remake of the series.<br /><br />Danielle's love for Starfield is sort of violated when the teenage idol, the heartthrob Darien Freeman is casted as the lead in the remake of the original series. She feels like her fandom is violated because Darien comes along with an entire fandom of teenage girls who are in love with him and his looks but not the Starfield fandom, they know nothing about it other than the fact that Darien Freeman is now cast in it. I must say if I was in Elle’s place I would feel the same way and turns out so does everyone else in the original Starfield fandom. The original series wasn't all that popular but it still gathered quite the cult following and these people were like family joined by their mutual love for Starfield and they all felt a surge of rage when Darien and his followers who knew nothing about this amazing series just invaded their sanctuary.<br /><br />But the poor guy however heart stoppingly handsome he is, is just a geek at heart. He does love his fame but for that fame he hides the part of him that knows everything about Starfield and is a fanboy. There's actually a point in the book where his internal monologue is - <i>”don't fanboy don’t fanboy”</i>, we can all relate to that. <br /><br />I feel the need to mention Darien's appearance on the show <i>Hello America</i>. Elle is watching the show host asking Darien the questions and he answers all of them but misses a question, not because he didn't know the answer but because his script told him to not answer so that he doesn't seem too geeky to the crowd, but as Elle doesn't know that and it increases her initial contempt towards the man who seems to be hijacking her most beloved series. I'm not sure why this incident stuck with me, but watching Darien after the show thinking back to how he hated that he couldn't answer a question he knew the answer to, really touched my heart.<br />.<br />Elle’s father started ExcelsiCon a convention for people in fandoms. Once he died Elle was left with a stepmother and two stepsisters who she couldn’t hate more. Watching Elle remember how her stepmother got rid of everything that belonged to her father was so sad and watching her stepmother take advantage of her at every turn, treat her like a slave has my blood boiling.<br />But this time she is not going to abide by the constriction her stepmother set for her. She is going to go to ExcelsiCon and take part in the cosplay event and hopefully win. <br /><br />Darien tries to contact the person who started ExcelsiCon unaware of the fact that he had died and his phone passed on to his daughter, Elle. They start talking to each other via text and start falling in love without ever having met. Darien loves talking to her because with her he doesn’t have to hide his inner geek and can just be who he is.<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>”I’m glad to share this sky with you —Maybe we should start looking up together, ah’blena.”</b>
</i><br /><br />I understand exactly why their conversations were so dear to each other, they were an escape from each of their lives into a discussion about the story they care about most as neither of them has anyone else to share their love for the fandom. I can't imagine not having someone to go crazy and fangirl with. In fact my best friend is the one who pushed me to read this book because she finished it recently and loved it. She was right, this was an amazing read.<br /><br />As long as you are a reader and a fangirl/boy I feel like this book is right up your alley. The fandom aspect was so perfectly incorporated into the retelling it feels absolutely perfect. This book proves how your fandom can be your family and watching both of the characters find solace in that is heartwarming.<br /><br />Everyone in the fandom are people that understood how supportive characters and stories can be in a person's life. All stories teach us to grow as people and we are constantly learning things from stories we could never have learnt otherwise. They give us hope and they allow us to dream and the people who remain ignorant of the power fiction possesses shall never know the joy that it is to see past reality into worlds that will never exist but will always have a place in our hearts.<br /><br /><i>
  <b> Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite</b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="7658723500234589556" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1929768303" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1929768303" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1929768303?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=retellings">retellings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1929768303" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5082324764933594794"><i>ARC provided by the publisher via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/>This was so surprisingly delightful, and made me so unexpectedly emotional. Everyone knows the story of <i>Cinderella</i>, but this modern day retelling feels and was actually able to evoke quite the feelings from me. This is a heartwarming story and if you consider yourself nerdy whatsoever, don't let this book pass you by. <br/><br/>I obviously feel confident saying I'm a pretty geeky individual: <br/>➽ <b>Video Games?</b> I've been raiding for o</span>
  <span id="freeText5082324764933594794" style="display:none"><i>ARC provided by the publisher via Netgalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>This was so surprisingly delightful, and made me so unexpectedly emotional. Everyone knows the story of <i>Cinderella</i>, but this modern day retelling feels and was actually able to evoke quite the feelings from me. This is a heartwarming story and if you consider yourself nerdy whatsoever, don't let this book pass you by. <br><br>I obviously feel confident saying I'm a pretty geeky individual: <br>➽ <b>Video Games?</b> I've been raiding for over 10 years in <i>World of Warcraft</i>.<br>➽ <b>Esports?</b> <i>League of Legends</i> is my world, and I will not miss NA LCS or LCK for anything. <br>➽ <b>D&amp;D?</b> Vox Machina is love, Vox Machina is life. #Critters<br>➽ <b>Fandoms?</b> You all know I have that covered. <i>*Explains why Hermione and Draco should have been together*</i><br>➽ <b>Cons?</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449513224i/17295245._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've embraced and been comfortable with my nerdiness for a while now, but it wasn't always so easy, and this book really struck a chord with me and what I felt like when I was seventeen years old and still unsure of who I was. This book truly felt like my coming of age story, and a book that would have meant everything to me if I would have picked it up when I was younger and needed it. For that alone I will always cherish this story and recommend this book. <br><br>Never be ashamed of who you are or what you love. Celebrate your passions loudly and unapologetically. Never settle and never listen to anyone who wants you to become something you're not. I promise you, there is someone out there who will love and accept you for who you are and will care about what you love. In the mean time, love yourself and embrace what you love. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m the lost princess. I’m the villain of my story, and the hero. Part of my mom and part of my dad. I am a fact of the universe. The Possible and the Impossible. I am not no one.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> Okay, I promise I'll try to be less emotional. This adorable story starts out like any modern day <i>Cinderella</i> retelling would: with a girl grieving the loss of her father, while trying to put up with her evil stepmother, while dealing with her evil stepsisters. She feels alone and so isolated, while trying to keep the peace and do all the housework and chores for her unloving family. If only there was a way for her to escape.<br><br>Our <i>Cinderella</i>, Elle, escapes the only way she knows how: in the fandom of the beloved sci-fi show that she shared with her father, Starfield! Starfield is much like a mix of <i>Star Trek</i> and <i>Star Wars</i>, and it just so happens that the show is getting remade into a movie and Elle's favorite character is being played by the most unexpected of male leads. Oh, and Elle also runs a Starfield blog, where she voices her opinion of the casting choices.<br><br>Meanwhile, this male lead, Darien, is dealing with his own broken home, even though Hollywood makes everything appear perfect on the outside. Even though he's supposed to just be a teen heartthrob, he is secretly obsessed with Starfield and has dreamed of this leading role his whole life. <br><br>Then, due to a very strange set of events and miscommunication, our two protagonists start texting one another, while being completely unaware of whom they are actually communicating with. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I hide the phone under my pillow. Because I’m not a princess. And this is the impossible universe, where nothing good ever happens.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Throw in a cosplay ball, a food truck pumpkin, an amazing friend, and endless geeky references and you have yourself this amazing story wrapped up with helpful discussions and wonderful reminders to love yourself and know your worth. <br><br>There is also amazing lesbian representation in this book. The story doesn't shy away from it what so ever, and it is treated, as it should be treated, like normal. Again, this book is important, needed, and truly a shining light in 2017 publications. <br><br>This book was pure joy to read, and I connected with it on a very deep level. This story is truly a love letter to fandoms in general, and it warmed my heart to no end. I was laughing, crying, smiling, and absolutely loving this book from cover to cover. I am so happy a book like this is getting published, and I wish it all the success in the world. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany/profile" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a><br><br><i>The quotes above were taken from an ARC and are subject to change upon publication.</i> </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2054894639" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1643805085137320311">THIS BOOK WAS EVERYTHING.<br/><br/>Well I wasn't expecting to finish this book four hours after I started it but here we are. I loved EVERYTHING about this book. The nerdiness. The cons. The CHARACTERS. Basically it took my favorite things from other Cinderella retellings and wrapped them into one, PLUS EVEN MORE.<br/>I love that it's told from dual perspective and tackles (even in passing) issues like "fake geek girls" and people not understanding how much you love something that's nerdy and your favorite thi</span>
  <span id="freeText1643805085137320311" style="display:none">THIS BOOK WAS EVERYTHING.<br /><br />Well I wasn't expecting to finish this book four hours after I started it but here we are. I loved EVERYTHING about this book. The nerdiness. The cons. The CHARACTERS. Basically it took my favorite things from other Cinderella retellings and wrapped them into one, PLUS EVEN MORE.<br />I love that it's told from dual perspective and tackles (even in passing) issues like "fake geek girls" and people not understanding how much you love something that's nerdy and your favorite thing being rebooted or turned into a movie. <br />I didn't love that most of the "evil" characters were women (though one was a guy!) but that's kinda cinderella for you.<br />Gosh I cried throughout this book and just felt a lot of it deep in my heart. I love things so deeply and people don't understand and this book took that and was like that's your strength and I JUST I'm getting emotional again probably because I need to sleep.<br />This book was everything to me that's it ok goodnight.<br /><br />Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite.</span>

<div id="review_2431640800" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2431640800" />
    <a title="Miranda Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads"><img alt="Miranda Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592243041p2/71848701.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2431640800?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miranda Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miranda Reads" href="/user/show/71848701-miranda-reads">Miranda Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/71848701-miranda-reads?shelf=digitallibrary">digitallibrary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2431640800" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3047439149362786291"><blockquote>
<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1591583386i/29611785._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='225' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The <b><u> <a href='https://youtu.be/CD3ZxQtLtl0' rel='nofollow noopener'>May Reading Vlog</a></u></b> (aka tier listing 30+ books) is up! Now that you know where this one ranks, click the link to check out the rest! </blockquote><b>
  <u>The Written Review</u>
</b><blockquote>
<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1591846033i/29627198._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite.</i>
</blockquote>Elle Wittimer loves, loves, loves Starfield - it has all the best elements of all the best fandoms. <br/><br/>Her late mother and father both loved it, and her father was the man behind the convention for Starfield.<br/><br/>Currently, Elle lives with her Step-mom and twin step-siblings and to put it frank, they're making <b>he</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3047439149362786291" style="display:none"><blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1591583386i/29611785._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The <b><u> <a href="https://youtu.be/CD3ZxQtLtl0" rel="nofollow noopener">May Reading Vlog</a></u></b> (aka tier listing 30+ books) is up! Now that you know where this one ranks, click the link to check out the rest! </blockquote><b>
  <u>The Written Review</u>
</b><blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1591846033i/29627198._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite.</i>
</blockquote>Elle Wittimer loves, loves, loves Starfield - it has all the best elements of all the best fandoms. <br><br>Her late mother and father both loved it, and her father was the man behind the convention for Starfield.<br><br>Currently, Elle lives with her Step-mom and twin step-siblings and to put it frank, they're making <b>her life a living hell. </b><br><br>Then, she sees the announcement for Starfield's reboot as a movie series plus a costume contest at this year's ExcelsiCon, and she knows <b>she has to enter.</b><br><br>Darien Freeman - teenage heartthrob - is far more geek than anyone could've expected.<br><br>Before the <b>fame and fortune</b>, he was a lonely kid with absentee parents. And Starfield was his lifeline. <br><br>Now that he's the star of the upcoming movie, he is feeling all of the pressure from the media to get this exactly right.<br><br>When a fiery blog post (written under Elle's pseudonym) goes viral, Darien finds himself more lost than ever regarding his place in this fandom.<br><br>By chance, he texted Elle and she responded. Slowly, only through text, the two of them get closer. But with the Con, the movie and above all Elle's family keeping them apart, this is going to be one hellova costume contest. <blockquote>
  <i>Because in the end we're all just a bunch of weirdos standing in front of other weirdos, asking for their username.</i>
</blockquote>Omg. Yes. <br><br>This one hit me in the feels. <br><br>I absolutely<b> LOVED </b>the way Poston took the Cinderella trope and turned it around. It was so well done and so fresh.<br><br>Elle and Darien were such <b>great main characters</b>, I felt for both of them and truly loved all of the cutsey moments.<br><br>I also was impressed by the step-mother's commitment for evil. It was over the top and completely unreasonable, and yet it also felt realistic.<br><br>All in all, I LOVED this one and I cannot wait to get my hands on the next.</span>

          </span>

        <a title="sam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="sam" href="/user/show/53964123-sam">sam</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/53964123-sam?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1944151646" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4062468744973482817">Rating: 5⭐<br/>Reread update: I love this book sooo much! I thought I'd get bored during the reread but it wasn't like that at all. Read this if you haven't already.. Its bound to make you happy.<br/><br/>This book just made my favorites list. I usually don't read books from the contemporary genre but after reading this one I started experimenting with the genre more and realised, surprisingly, that I actually really enjoy it. If you have any problems with starting this genre like I did then definitely read th</span>
  <span id="freeText4062468744973482817" style="display:none">Rating: 5⭐<br />Reread update: I love this book sooo much! I thought I'd get bored during the reread but it wasn't like that at all. Read this if you haven't already.. Its bound to make you happy.<br /><br />This book just made my favorites list. I usually don't read books from the contemporary genre but after reading this one I started experimenting with the genre more and realised, surprisingly, that I actually really enjoy it. If you have any problems with starting this genre like I did then definitely read this book because it wont disappoint. This book had everything I absolutely would have wanted from a contemporary novel. The romance was absolutely sweet and adorable and heartwarming. I loved the way the author intricately wove the Cinderella elements into this story- with some twists obviously 😉. This was a modern day fairytale definitely worth every second of my time.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> "She wears life like Elvis wore sequins, with no apology laced into the seams.” </i>
</b><br /><br />This is a story about a girl named Danielle but everyone calls her Elle so you can too😁. She is a Starfield geek and literally lives for the fandom. She also has a not-so-popular blog called rebelgunner where she updates about fandom related news. After her dad aka the person who introduced her to the Starfield fandom and the founder of Excelsicon dies, Elle is victimized for loving Starfield and is surrounded by fake people who pretend to like it and know everything about it just because of Darien Freeman. This fact is taken personally by the entire fandom because for them, Starfield is their heart and soul.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> "You don’t put a soap opera star in charge of an entire galaxy.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Darien Freeman. Hollywood heartthrob and Carmindor in the remake of the Starfield series. He is also a major Starfield fanboy but he's not allowed to tell anyone. <br /><br />After an accidental texting mishap, a new sort of friendship blossoms between Elle and Darien with promise of something more and it watching it unfold was the most beautiful thing. <br /><br />A story about two teens trying to navigate life in their own ways and find comfort in each other with some added Hollywood and sisterly drama. A Cinderella story with a twist.<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite.” </i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_2334025708" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2334025708" />
    <a title="megs_bookrack" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack"><img alt="megs_bookrack" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532027727p2/48328025.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2334025708?book_show_action=true">Dec 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="megs_bookrack" class="user" itemprop="url" name="megs_bookrack" href="/user/show/48328025-megs-bookrack">megs_bookrack</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781455116379" href="/book/show/34352860-geekerella">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2334025708" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15979227804259284946">I'm a <b>geek</b> and I loved this book.<br/><br/>What else can I say?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577831986ra/28695382.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was my last completed book of 2019. <br/><br/>A excellent way to end a great reading year!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514717953ra/24805396.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>During the course of my 2019 Christmas holiday travels, I found myself alone in the car, <b>A LOT</b>. I wanted a little romance to keep me alert whilst driving. Not for me, of course, but on audio. <br/><br/>I had been putting this off forever, for unknown and totally irrelevant reasons, and on a whim decided to download it.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590542408ra/29547239.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The stars blessed me that day, as I found so much mo</span>
  <span id="freeText15979227804259284946" style="display:none">I'm a <b>geek</b> and I loved this book.<br><br>What else can I say?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1577831986ra/28695382.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was my last completed book of 2019. <br><br>A excellent way to end a great reading year!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1514717953ra/24805396.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>During the course of my 2019 Christmas holiday travels, I found myself alone in the car, <b>A LOT</b>. I wanted a little romance to keep me alert whilst driving. Not for me, of course, but on audio. <br><br>I had been putting this off forever, for unknown and totally irrelevant reasons, and on a whim decided to download it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590542408ra/29547239.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The stars blessed me that day, as I found so much more in this story than romance. <br><br>It genuinely touched my nerdy soul. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578066549ra/28706144.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I felt filled to capacity with acceptance and understanding whilst listening to this modern-day <i>Cinderella</i> retelling. <br><br>At its heart, <b>a story about embracing your passions and never apologizing for who you are or what you love</b>. Something I am trying to work on myself.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578066549ra/28706145.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Our protagonist, Elle Wittimer, is a teen living with her Step-Mother and two Step-Sisters in South Carolina, and yes, you guessed it, the Steps are wicked!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578066549ra/28706146.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Elle tries to stay out of their way as much as possible. <br><br>She spends her summer days working in a food truck called the <i>Magic Pumpkin</i> and her nights blogging about her favorite fandom, <i>Starfield</i>, a classic scifi show that she has loved her whole life. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590542408ra/29547240.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Starfield</i> is the one thing that makes her still feel connected to her deceased parents, both huge fans.<br><br>When it is announced that <i>Starfield</i> is soon to get a movie reboot, Elle can't wait to see who they cast. As any superfan though, she's worried they're going to ruin it. <br><br>Do reboots or adaptations ever truly do justice for our fandoms?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493322402ra/22604237.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After teen heartthrob, Darien Freeman, is announced to be playing the pivotal role of Federation Prince Carmindor, Elle knows it is going to suck. What would he possibly know about <i>Starfield</i>? <br><br>She suspects all he knows are abs workouts and alarmingly charming smiles. Fueled by anger, she takes to the web and blogs what a travesty it is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578066549ra/28706149.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Darien Freeman is a fan however. Being cast as Carmindor has been a life-long dream for him, but he's been cast to play a particular part, not just in the movie, but in life. Bubble-headed playboy is his image and he is forced to stick with it.<br><br>Written off by the <i>Starfield</i> fanbase as a faker of the highest order, Darien finds himself frustrated and misunderstood. But what can he possibly do about it? He's trapped.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578066549ra/28706148.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Under the same stars, Elle feels trapped as well. Her Steps are downright cruel to her, but she has no means of retaliation or true escape. She feels powerless against them.<br><br>To promote the new movie, the Starfield execs plan a cosplay contest to be held at ExcelsiCon; the very same Con created by Elle's late father. She can't believe her luck and sees the grand prize, tickets to L.A., as her means of escape.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586090869ra/29236294.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Darien is not pleased when he discovers he will be forced to attend the Con. He used to love attending Cons, but to have to go and not be able to proclaim his love as a true fan feels stifling.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Reaching out to a phone number listed as info for ExcelsiCon, he ends up getting in touch with Elle, but neither knows who the other is. Thus begins their relationship, via texts, and their means of finding escape through one another <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1565706030ra/27986802.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the very first chapter, I fell for Elle and her story, hook, line and sinker. <br><br>The homage to the original tale of <i>Cinderella</i>, while bringing it fully into the 21st-century, was beautifully crafted. I loved all the little details and connections throughout the book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1586090869ra/29236295.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the synopsis states, this is also a love letter to nerd culture and for many of us, that means a lot. <br><br>To feel that we aren't alone and there are legions of people out there just like us, who love the same things, accept us and don't call us weird, it feels good.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1578066549ra/28706150.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, I was really damn impressed with this and hope to be picking up the next, <i>Once Upon a Con</i> installment soon! <br><br>Thank you, Ashley Poston, for writing this. It was absolutely wonderful!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519508650ra/25117232.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1988440486" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1988440486" />
    <a title="Mischenko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1194517-mischenko"><img alt="Mischenko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587209348p2/1194517.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1988440486?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mischenko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mischenko" href="/user/show/1194517-mischenko">Mischenko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781594749933" href="/book/show/34790383-geekerella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1194517-mischenko?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1988440486" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18242616860312257351">This is such a cute and clever story!<br/><br/>Ever since Elle was little, she’s loved a Sci-Fi TV series called <i>Starfield.</i> Her parents also loved the show and her dad actually started a convention called ExcelsiCon for the fans. Now, there’s a <i>Starfield</i> reboot with new actors and a chance to enter a cosplay contest. Winners of the contest will get a chance to attend the ExcelsiCon Ball and meet the new actor playing the part of Prince Carmindor. Elle knows she must enter the contest because she’s an ulti</span>
  <span id="freeText18242616860312257351" style="display:none">This is such a cute and clever story!<br /><br />Ever since Elle was little, she’s loved a Sci-Fi TV series called <i>Starfield.</i> Her parents also loved the show and her dad actually started a convention called ExcelsiCon for the fans. Now, there’s a <i>Starfield</i> reboot with new actors and a chance to enter a cosplay contest. Winners of the contest will get a chance to attend the ExcelsiCon Ball and meet the new actor playing the part of Prince Carmindor. Elle knows she must enter the contest because she’s an ultimate fangirl and lives for <i>Starfield</i>. The big problem is that Elle’s stepmother is bitter about anything that doesn’t benefit her and she hates <i>Starfield</i>. Elle will have to find a way to make this happen on her own and without her stepmom finding out.<br /><br /><br />Darien Freeman is a young actor who’s also a <i>Starfield</i> fan and he’s playing the star role as Prince Carmindor in the <i>Starfield reboot</i>. He’s become uncomfortable in this position because <i>Starfield</i> fans don’t seem to take him seriously. They think he’s a joke because of the previous show he starred in and don’t believe he’s a true <i>Starfield</i> fan. So now he wants to find a way to avoid the signing event at ExcelsiCon altogether, until he meets someone who helps him think otherwise. Will Darien be able to pull off the part and prove to everyone that he has what it takes to represent the original Carmindor?<br /><br />The story does follow similar tropes and themes from <i>Cinderella</i> including a horrible stepmother, stepsisters, and other not-so-great circumstances. Elle still mourns the loss of her father and due to how she’s treated by her evil family, she has fairly low self-esteem. Her stepsisters are the popular kids at school and Elle doesn’t have many friends. She works on a food truck called ‘The Magic Pumpkin’ along with a girl named Sage who she eventually becomes quite close to. Elle learns a lot about being herself throughout the book and also about the true definition of family and friendship. I could totally relate to Elle and she’s definitely a likeable character.<br /><br />I loved Sage! I think she turned out to be my favorite character. She’s exactly the kind of friend Elle needs. She’s strong, supportive, and teaches Elle to be herself and to be proud of who she is. Sage is different and isn’t afraid to express herself to anyone. This helps Elle tremendously, especially with her stepsisters, Chloe and Cal. I loved the way the author made these two sisters different with Chloe being the true evil one.<br /><br />As for Darien, I liked his character. There were parts in the book where I thought he was a little annoying and even cocky at times, but he’s dealing with his own set of struggles, including a dad who he’s not close to and a nonexistent mother. When Darien became an actor, his friends became distant and everything sort of fell apart, so he doesn’t have many friends at this point. As for the parents, I couldn’t stand them. Elle’s stepmom is horrible and treats her like garbage. Darien’s dad is pretty bad too and cares more about what’s best for himself than what’s best for Darien.<br /><br />Overall, I really enjoyed this retelling. I think the author was very creative with how she switched up the plot, setting, and characters. The writing is good and the pacing was spot on for me. I found some parts comical and even shed a few tears at other emotional parts regarding Elle and her dad. The ending was a little too cheesy for my taste and I didn’t like the way the characters came together, but I absolutely cannot deny that I was invested in these characters all the way to the end. Everytime I had to put the book down, I looked forward to picking it back up again.<br /><br />I think anyone who loves <i>Cinderella</i> retellings will enjoy this book. I’m looking forward to the next book.<br /><br />4****<br /><br />You can also read this review @<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.readrantrockandroll.com">www.readrantrockandroll.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18242616860312257351" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1967584900" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1967584900" />
    <a title="Cristina Monica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica"><img alt="Cristina Monica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589617514p2/14596170.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1967584900?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cristina Monica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cristina Monica" href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=cinderella">cinderella</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14596170-cristina-monica?shelf=fairy-tale-retellings">fairy-tale-retellings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1967584900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer465518154919630526">GEEKERELLA is a charming book very reminiscent of CINDER & ELLA. The similarities are evident, so if you’ve read that book, this one may not impress you, but still, it is a pleasant read.<br/><br/>It’s simply not my kind of read. Well I did enjoy it, because it’s close to impossible for me to dislike a fairytale retelling, though it’s definitely not the type of book I will want to reread in the future. <br/><br/>Because I just can’t believe in falling in love through the phone. There are certainly a lot of things y</span>
  <span id="freeText465518154919630526" style="display:none">GEEKERELLA is a charming book very reminiscent of CINDER &amp; ELLA. The similarities are evident, so if you’ve read that book, this one may not impress you, but still, it is a pleasant read.<br /><br />It’s simply not my kind of read. Well I did enjoy it, because it’s close to impossible for me to dislike a fairytale retelling, though it’s definitely not the type of book I will want to reread in the future. <br /><br />Because I just can’t believe in falling in love through the phone. There are certainly a lot of things you can do through the phone and with your phone, but literally falling in love with someone? <br /><br />Even if it were truly possible – which I dismiss as a possibility – I highly dislike the idea of it. You can’t ‘‘be there’’ for someone via your phone. It’s way too easy. ‘‘Being there for someone’’ requires more than you picking up the phone.<br /><br />But I am surprised with how the story unfolded. Having Darien (Prince Charming)’s point of views really brought something to the story. A celebrity falling in love with a common mortal is a bit of a cliché, but the author made Darien seem so normal that I had no trouble believing it. <br /><br />GEEKERELLA seems like a light, fun read. It has its fun moments – that’s true – and I’m not going to say it’s a dark, heavy read, but it does deal with loss and loneliness, which means that it’s not rainbows and sunshine everywhere. <br /><br />Basically, I’d recommend it if you’ve thoroughly enjoyed CINDER &amp; ELLA, or if you want to read a very contemporary retelling of CINDERELLA. <br /><br /><a href="https://hitormissbooks.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/c/LolaReviewer" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a>Twitter</a> | <a>Instagram</a> | <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/105021852309973899120/posts" rel="nofollow noopener">Google+</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/hit-miss-books-12564715" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="465518154919630526" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText5227884337432240075" style="display:none">gahhhhhh this book was so ... so... so... ummm what is the word?? CUTE (eww i hate that word). gah forget it this book made me smile. ME. Yes it was quite boring in the beginning but aaaahhhh it picks up and those little details connected to the original Cinderella story i was screaming throughout the book and telling my sister about the "Geek" twists. <br><br>🌟 So what's this about? Well we have <b>Elle</b> a girl grieving the loss of her father, while trying to put up with her evil stepmother and dealing with her evil stepsisters. And she escapes all of this by fangirling and geeking over <b>Starfield</b> (tbh i would watch that damned show if it was real) and we have <b>Darien</b> he's... even though he's supposed to just be a teen heartthrob, he is secretly obsessed with Starfield and has dreamed of this leading role his whole life. And then due to some miscommunications our MC's start texting each other. Throw in a Pumpkin Truck, an awesome best friend, the best cosplay ball and voila!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494730735i/22744405._SX540_.jpg" width="1000" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>🌟 That cosplay scene?     <a title="Emer (A Little Haze)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4629647-emer-a-little-haze"><img alt="Emer (A Little Haze)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589390599p2/4629647.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1947722220?book_show_action=true">May 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emer (A Little Haze)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emer (A Little Haze)" href="/user/show/4629647-emer-a-little-haze">Emer (A Little Haze)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/33224718-geekerella">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=1star">1star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=the-hype-lies">the-hype-lies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=read2017">read2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4629647-emer-a-little-haze?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1947722220" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11179744537963828634">My feelings while reading this book can best be explained by what this guy just went through:<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494375721ra/22709124.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OUCH!!!!<br/><br/>Oh gosh this was painful! To start with the writing felt very stilted to me. There was no easy flow. It read quite awkwardly I thought. The main characters in the book all had a sort of pantomime-esque vibe going on that also really didn't work for me. This was supposed to be a contemporary right?? Therefore, you'd think that some realism was required!!! And overall it was just an incredibly unim</span>
  <span id="freeText11179744537963828634" style="display:none">My feelings while reading this book can best be explained by what this guy just went through:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494375721ra/22709124.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OUCH!!!!<br><br>Oh gosh this was painful! To start with the writing felt very stilted to me. There was no easy flow. It read quite awkwardly I thought. The main characters in the book all had a sort of pantomime-esque vibe going on that also really didn't work for me. This was supposed to be a contemporary right?? Therefore, you'd think that some realism was required!!! And overall it was just an incredibly unimaginative retelling of a time-honoured classic. It followed the fairytale to a fault and, therefore, instead of breathing new life into the Cinderella storyline, it just felt boringly predictable. <br>Dull dull dull dull!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494374669ra/22709058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Such a shame. This sounded like it could have been super cute, but that's one of the biggest problems with fairytale retellings I guess. How close do you go to the source material? <br>This one was much too close and then even the <i>slight</i> differences felt jaded... <br>I don't know if anyone else can recall that Hilary Duff teen Cinderella film from the early 2000s: A Cinderella Story. It had that Lucas guy from One Tree Hill in it too... This novel almost felt like fan-fic version of that film to me. <br>I don't know... Maybe Cinderella is just too well known... <br><br>This book needed a twist. Something to make it stand out. Perhaps something to make it a little grittier and have less of the over-the-top ridiculousness with the characterisations of the main characters. Sadly, as I said before, it was just soooo freaking dull!!!!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1494374669ra/22709059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh I'm probably just too old for this anyway... Time to just forget this and move on to my next read. Although I'm really getting tired of these low ratings... <br>But here we go again... <b><br>one star</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17537398268564663009"><b>5 Geeky Starfield Stars 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟</b><br/><br/>This book was just SO adorable!<br/><br/>I am not a super fan of anything or part of any type of fandom.... especially not anything involving the word star.... but that did not matter at all this book was a lot of fun.... a very well done retelling of Cinderella with a modern twist...right down to the pumpkin food truck....<br/><br/>Elle was such a fabulously likable character.... even though she and my teenage self had very little in common I still found her so Real and relatable.... D</span>
  <span id="freeText17537398268564663009" style="display:none"><b>5 Geeky Starfield Stars 🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟</b><br /><br />This book was just SO adorable!<br /><br />I am not a super fan of anything or part of any type of fandom.... especially not anything involving the word star.... but that did not matter at all this book was a lot of fun.... a very well done retelling of Cinderella with a modern twist...right down to the pumpkin food truck....<br /><br />Elle was such a fabulously likable character.... even though she and my teenage self had very little in common I still found her so Real and relatable.... Darien, well what’s not to like.... a super hot movie star with abs of steel and a heart of gold.... although my favorite character has to be Sage she was the most unlikely perfect ferry godmother....<br /><br /> I would strongly recommend this book to everybody who believes in happily ever after.... when you’re in the mood for a fun fluffy fairytale with a side of nerd....<br /><br /><br />🎧🎧🎧 Narration: was very well done by both narrators, however there were a few mishaps with the editing... some lines repeated enough that I noticed and I am not necessarily one to notice those things....<br /><br />📚🌹 find all my reviews on our lovely blog <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://audiokilledthebookmark.com/">https://audiokilledthebookmark.com/</a></span>

<div id="review_2081117742" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2081117742" />
    <a title="Bonnie Shores" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25177308-bonnie-shores"><img alt="Bonnie Shores" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500403398p2/25177308.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2081117742?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bonnie Shores" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bonnie Shores" href="/user/show/25177308-bonnie-shores">Bonnie Shores</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25177308-bonnie-shores?shelf=geek-love">geek-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2081117742" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6625475101539734711">I <b>
  <i>LOVED</i>
</b> this book soooooooooooo much!!!😍 I mean, I totally identified with Elle and her devotion to <i>Starfield</i>, the short-lived TV series that spawned a generation of superfans (which is exactly what happened with <b>Star Trek</b>, my first—and still—love).<br/><a href='http://imgur.com/Nt89GRd' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1503006258i/23619935._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>I jumped at the opportunity to visit a Star Trek Enterprise replica set and totally geeked out with other fans. (above) I even attended the San Diego ComicCon a couple of years ago and snapped a quick pic with a Captain Kirk wannabe. I, howeve</span>
  <span id="freeText6625475101539734711" style="display:none">I <b>
  <i>LOVED</i>
</b> this book soooooooooooo much!!!😍 I mean, I totally identified with Elle and her devotion to <i>Starfield</i>, the short-lived TV series that spawned a generation of superfans (which is exactly what happened with <b>Star Trek</b>, my first—and still—love).<br><a href="http://imgur.com/Nt89GRd" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1503006258i/23619935._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I jumped at the opportunity to visit a Star Trek Enterprise replica set and totally geeked out with other fans. (above) I even attended the San Diego ComicCon a couple of years ago and snapped a quick pic with a Captain Kirk wannabe. I, however, remain devoted to Mr. Spock, hence, my blue uniform. Alas, I didn't see a Spock anywhere. <i>Live long and prosper.</i> 🖖<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/6kl3Jfr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1503006740i/23619970._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But I digress... This is the story of <s>Cinderella</s>, ahem, Geekerella, Elle, whose father (and mother) was such a fan of <i>Starfield</i> that he started his own convention, ExcelsiCon, in honor of his favorite show.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Look to the stars. Aim. Ignite.”</i>
</b><br><br>Elle's dad died, though, when she was only eight years old and she's been living with her stepmother and two stepsisters who defintely don't understand her continued obsession with <i>Starfield</i>.<br><br>When she receives a phone call from an unknown number asking about ExcelsiCon (which had become huge), she doesn't think much of it. After all, with her dad (and mom) long gone, this is a subject that still causes her heart to break. She had attended the Con with her dad and knew it intimately. She had even danced around her livingroom in her mom's cosplay gown. But those times were over and she was just trying to get through life.<br><br>Unbeknownst to Elle, the unknown number was Darien Freeman, the teen heartthrob who had been cast as Prince Carmindor in the upcoming <i>Starfield</i> movie. Bored one night, and still trying to get out of his appearance at ExcelsiCon, Darien texts Elle again and thus begins their friendship.<br><br>I don't want to give anything else away but, obviously, this is a retelling of Cinderella and it follows the same basic story line. Ashley Poston does a fantastic job of updating this beloved tale and putting her own unique and very creative spin on it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503008824ra/23620181.gif" width="500" height="279" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is just the most adorable story and it made me really happy! 😊</span>
  <a data-text-id="6625475101539734711" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
